# 分析流程 {#abstract}

## 需求

通过软件预测甲基化调控因子（如METTL14）的靶基因，并通过数据库筛选于PCOS患者中表达水平具有显著差异性的基因，合并交集，并对该交集中的基因进行功能富集和KEGG通路富集分析，筛选PCOS患者中可能的METTL14甲基化调控基因及其相关通路；

## 实际流程

从 EpiFactors 获取表观遗传调控因子，筛出甲基化相关调控因子  (A 集合) 。
获取 PCOS GEO 数据，差异分析得到 DEGs，发现可能存在甲基化修饰位点的基因 B 集合。
在 PCOS 中筛选出差异表达的甲基化调控因子 (C集合) ，与 B 集合关联分析，随后富集分析。

补充了显著关联的基因的 PTMs 预测 (组蛋白修饰位点预测，包括 Methylarginine，Methyllysine 类型。



# 材料和方法 {#introduction}

## 数据分析平台

在 Linux pop-os x86_64 (6.9.3-76060903-generic) 上，使用 R version 4.4.2 (2024-10-31) (https://www.r-project.org/) 对数据统计分析与整合分析。


##  EpiFactors 表观遗传调控因子数据获取 (Dataset: METHY)

从数据库 `EpiFactors` (2023, **IF:16.6**, Q1, Nucleic acids research)[@Epifactors2022Maraku2023] 获取表观遗传调控蛋白的数据。

##  GEO 数据获取 (Dataset: PCOS)

以 R 包 `GEOquery` (2.74.0) 获取 GSE277906 数据集。

##  Limma 差异分析 (Dataset: PCOS)

以 R 包 `limma` (3.62.1) (2005, **IF:**, , )[@LimmaLinearMSmyth2005] `edgeR` (4.4.0) (, **IF:**, , )[@EdgerDifferenChen] 进行差异分析。以 `edgeR::filterByExpr` 过滤 count 数量小于 10 的基因。以 `edgeR::calcNormFactors`，`limma::voom` 转化 count 数据为 log2 counts-per-million (logCPM)。分析方法参考 <https://bioconductor.org/packages/release/workflows/vignettes/RNAseq123/inst/doc/limmaWorkflow.html>。随后，以 公式 ~ 0 + group 创建设计矩阵 (design matrix) 用于线性分析。
使用 `limma::lmFit`, `limma::contrasts.fit`, `limma::eBayes` 差异分析对比组：pcos vs control。以 `limma::topTable` 提取所有结果，并过滤得到 P.Value 小于 0.05，|Log2(FC)| 大于 0.5 的统计结果。
对 GSE277906 的 mRNA 数据 (protein_coding) 差异分析

##  富集分析 (Dataset: SIGCOR_05)

以 ClusterProfiler R 包 (4.15.0.2) (2021, **IF:33.2**, Q1, The Innovation)[@ClusterprofilerWuTi2021]进行 KEGG 和 GO 富集分析。
以 `pathview` R 包 (1.46.0) 对选择的 KEGG 通路可视化。

##  MusiteDeep 蛋白质转录后修饰位点预测 (Dataset: SIGCOR_05)

以 `biomaRt` (2009, **IF:13.1**, Q1, Nature protocols)[@MappingIdentifDurinc2009] 获取蛋白质 (hsa) 的序列 (`biomaRt::getSequence` 获取 peptide)。
以 Python 工具 `MusiteDeep` (2020, **IF:16.6**, Q1, Nucleic Acids Research)[@MusitedeepADWang2020] 预测 Methylarginine, Methyllysine 修饰位点，设定 PTM 得分截断为 0.5。

##  富集分析 (Dataset: PTMS)

以 ClusterProfiler R 包 (4.15.0.2) (2021, **IF:33.2**, Q1, The Innovation)[@ClusterprofilerWuTi2021]进行 KEGG 和 GO 富集分析。
以 `pathview` R 包 (1.46.0) 对选择的 KEGG 通路可视化。

# 分析结果 {#workflow}

## EpiFactors 表观遗传调控因子数据获取 (METHY)

从所有 表观调控因子 Fig. `<w:hyperlink w:anchor="Distribution-all-protein-of-epigenetic-regulators"><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="begin" w:dirty="true"/></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:instrText xml:space="preserve" w:dirty="true"> REF Distribution-all-protein-of-epigenetic-regulators \h</w:instrText></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="end" w:dirty="true"/></w:r></w:hyperlink>`{=openxml}

## GEO 数据获取 (PCOS)

获取 GEO PCOS 数据，用于筛选差异表达基因。




- Data Source ID: GSE277906
- data_processing: Illumina Casava1.7 software used for basecalling.
- data_processing.1: Raw reads of fastq format were firstly processed using fastp and the low quality reads were removed to obtain the clean reads.
- data_processing.2: The clean reads were mapped to the reference genome using HISAT2. FPKM of each gene was calculated and the read counts of each gene were obtained by HTSeq-count
- data_processing.3: Assembly: GRCh38
- (Others): ...
```{=openxml}
<w:p><w:pPr><w:pStyle w:val="Normal"/><w:jc w:val="center"/><w:pBdr><w:bottom w:val="none" w:sz="0" w:space="0" w:color="000000"/><w:top w:val="none" w:sz="0" w:space="0" w:color="000000"/><w:left w:val="none" w:sz="0" w:space="0" w:color="000000"/><w:right w:val="none" w:sz="0" w:space="0" w:color="000000"/></w:pBdr><w:spacing w:after="0" w:before="0" w:line="480"/><w:ind w:left="0" w:right="0" w:firstLine="0" w:firstLineChars="0"/></w:pPr><w:r><w:rPr><w:rFonts/><w:b w:val="true"/></w:rPr><w:t xml:space="preserve">(见Figure+Table/PCOS-GSE277906-content)</w:t></w:r></w:p>
```


## 差异表达的 Methylation Factors

将差异表达基因与  Tab. `<w:hyperlink w:anchor="METHY-regulators"><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="begin" w:dirty="true"/></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:instrText xml:space="preserve" w:dirty="true"> REF METHY-regulators \h</w:instrText></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="end" w:dirty="true"/></w:r></w:hyperlink>`{=openxml} 中的因子取交集，
见 Fig. `<w:hyperlink w:anchor="Intersection-of-Methy-factor-with-DEGs"><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="begin" w:dirty="true"/></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:instrText xml:space="preserve" w:dirty="true"> REF Intersection-of-Methy-factor-with-DEGs \h</w:instrText></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="end" w:dirty="true"/></w:r></w:hyperlink>`{=openxml} 。

## Methylation Factors 与 DEGs 关联分析

为了寻找 Fig. `<w:hyperlink w:anchor="Intersection-of-Methy-factor-with-DEGs"><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="begin" w:dirty="true"/></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:instrText xml:space="preserve" w:dirty="true"> REF Intersection-of-Methy-factor-with-DEGs \h</w:instrText></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="end" w:dirty="true"/></w:r></w:hyperlink>`{=openxml}  中发现的差异表达的 Methylation Factors 
可能调控的 DEGs 修饰，将两个数据集作关联分析，结果见 Tab. `<w:hyperlink w:anchor="All-correlation-results"><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="begin" w:dirty="true"/></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:instrText xml:space="preserve" w:dirty="true"> REF All-correlation-results \h</w:instrText></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="end" w:dirty="true"/></w:r></w:hyperlink>`{=openxml} 。

# 总结 {#conclusion}

筛选的甲基化调控因子为 PRDM6，可能调控的基因见 Tab. `<w:hyperlink w:anchor="correlation-results-05"><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="begin" w:dirty="true"/></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:instrText xml:space="preserve" w:dirty="true"> REF correlation-results-05 \h</w:instrText></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="end" w:dirty="true"/></w:r></w:hyperlink>`{=openxml} ，
富集分析结果中，cAMP 通路最为显著，Fig. `<w:hyperlink w:anchor="SIGCOR-05-hsa04024-visualization"><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="begin" w:dirty="true"/></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:instrText xml:space="preserve" w:dirty="true"> REF SIGCOR-05-hsa04024-visualization \h</w:instrText></w:r><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships" xmlns:w14="http://schemas.microsoft.com/office/word/2010/wordml"><w:rPr/><w:fldChar w:fldCharType="end" w:dirty="true"/></w:r></w:hyperlink>`{=openxml} 。

cAMP 通路的三个基因的修饰位点见 Fig. `<w:hyperlink w:anchor="SIGCOR-05-RAC3-PTM-score"><w:r xmlns:w="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/wordprocessingml/2006/main" xmlns:wp="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/drawingml/2006/wordprocessingDrawing" xmlns:r="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/officeDocument/2006/relationships"
